Optimization Algorithms for Joint OFDM Waveform Design and RIS Configuration in 6G Networks: From Convex Relaxation to Foundation Models
Authors: Ahmet Kaplan
First: 2026-06-30T08:34:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-30T08:34:46+00:00
Comments: 22 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Joint OFDM-RIS optimization for 6G is a mixed-integer nonlinear programming (MINLP) problem covering sum-rate maximization, energy efficiency, max-min fairness, and peak-to-average power ratio (PAPR)-constrained objectives. Seventy-eight joint OFDM-RIS optimization works published between 2021 and 2026 are surveyed. No standardized benchmark exists, and cross-paper comparisons remain infeasible. This survey classifies these works into four paradigms: (I) model-based convex relaxation, (II) heuristic and metaheuristic search, (III) deep reinforcement and unsupervised learning, and (IV) emerging methods including foundation models (FM), diffusion-based generative AI, and quantum optimization. A literature synthesis of self-reported benchmarks shows that ML-based methods (Paradigm~III) report 95-99\% of model-based spectral efficiency at 10^2-10^4 x faster per-inference runtime (method-pair dependent; literature values are self-reported and exclude ML pre-training cost). A companion tutorial benchmark at N=16, N=64, and N=128 reveals a critical scaling property: GPU-based neural network inference (DDQN, PPO, graph neural network (GNN), unsupervised DL) is N-invariant, with identical runtime at N=16 and N=128, while iterative solvers (AO+SCA, PSO) scale polynomially. Energy efficiency (P2) and PAPR-constrained (P4) benchmarks are deferred to future work with standardized power models and waveform generators. Six open challenges emerge from the synthesis: the cross-paradigm benchmark deficit, real-world hardware-constrained deployment, joint waveform-RIS optimization for doubly-dispersive channels, multi-objective PAPR trade-offs, LLM safety in live network control, and diminishing returns of standalone heuristics. We specify requirements for a standardized benchmark. This study serves as a roadmap for researchers and practitioners working on joint OFDM-RIS optimization in 6G networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：6G网络中联合OFDM波形设计和RIS配置的优化算法：从凸松弛到基础模型
6G中的联合OFDM-RIS优化是一个混合整数非线性规划（MINLP）问题，涵盖了总速率最大化、能量效率、最大-最小公平性和峰值-平均功率比（PAPR）约束目标。调查了2021年至2026年间发表的78项联合OFDM-RIS优化工作。尚无标准化基准，跨论文比较仍不可行。本调查将这些工作分为四种范式：（I）基于模型的凸松弛，（II）启发式和元启发式搜索，（III）深度强化和无监督学习，以及（IV）包括基础模型（FM）、基于扩散的生成AI和量子优化的新兴方法。自报告基准的文献综合显示，基于机器学习的方法（范式III）在每次推理运行时间上以10^2-10^4倍的速度报告95-99%的基于模型的光谱效率（方法对依赖；文献值为自报告且不包括机器学习预训练成本）。在N=16、N=64和N=128的伴随教程基准中揭示了一个关键的缩放特性：基于GPU的神经网络推理（DDQN、PPO、图神经网络（GNN）、无监督深度学习）是N不变的，在N=16和N=128时具有相同的运行时间，而迭代求解器（AO+SCA、PSO）则呈多项式缩放。能量效率（P2）和PAPR约束（P4）基准推迟到未来工作，需使用标准化功率模型和波形生成器。从综合中出现六个开放挑战：跨范式基准缺口、现实世界硬件受限的部署、双散射信道的联合波形-RIS优化、多目标PAPR权衡、LLM在实时网络控制中的安全性，以及独立启发式的收益递减。我们为标准化基准指定了要求。本研究为在6G网络中从事联合OFDM-RIS优化的研究人员和从业者提供了路线图。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the optimization of joint OFDM-RIS in 6G networks, highlighting the lack of standardized benchmarks and the challenges in cross-paper comparisons. Previous methods include model-based convex relaxation, heuristic searches, and machine learning approaches, each with limitations such as inefficiency or lack of scalability. The proposed approach introduces a comprehensive survey of 78 optimization works and classifies them into four paradigms, emphasizing the advantages of machine learning methods that achieve high spectral efficiency with significantly faster runtimes. The paper contributes by identifying six open challenges in the field and proposing a roadmap for future research, while the methodology involves a literature synthesis and benchmarking across various paradigms. The findings indicate that machine learning-based methods can achieve 95-99% of the efficiency of traditional methods while being orders of magnitude faster, supporting the goal of improving joint OFDM-RIS optimization.
本文探讨了6G网络中联合OFDM-RIS配置的优化，强调了标准化基准缺失及现有研究比较的挑战。以往的方法，包括基于模型的凸松弛和启发式方法，在可扩展性和效率上存在局限，而提出的方法则结合了基础模型和生成性人工智能等新兴技术，以提升性能。本文对78项优化工作进行了全面调查，将其分类为四种范式，并揭示了基于机器学习的方法在光谱效率上达到传统方法的95-99%，但推理时间显著更快。研究方法包括文献综合和教程基准，展示了GPU基础的神经网络推理的N不变性，相较于迭代求解器的多项式扩展，识别出未来研究中的六个开放挑战。
Robust Harmful Features Under Jailbreak Attacks: Mechanistic Evidence from Attention Head Specialization in Large Language Models
Authors: Yanchen Yin, Dongqi Han, Linghui Li
Venue: ICML 2026 Oral presentation
First: 2026-06-26T14:51:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-29T15:00:34+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 19 figures. Accepted at ICML 2026 as an Oral presentation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks bypass LLM safety alignment, yet their mechanisms remain poorly understood. We provide evidence that attacks do not comprehensively eliminate safety features, but instead selectively suppress specific attention heads. We identify two functionally differentiated types: Adversarially Compromised Heads (ACHs) concentrated in early layers, which are suppressed under attacks, and Safety-Aligned Heads (SAHs) in mid-layers, which maintain robust activations even when attacks succeed. Ablation studies support the causal role of ACHs and the contribution of SAHs to robust activations: suppressing a small number of ACHs is sufficient to induce jailbreak-like behavior on normally refused inputs, while removing SAHs substantially weakens mid-layer safety activations. Token-level attribution further shows that ACH suppression is driven specifically by attack-template tokens, providing a mechanistic account of why attacks can bypass refusal decisions through ACH suppression while leaving internal safety signals sustained by SAHs -- a phenomenon we term Robust Harmful Features. To validate the practical significance of this robustness, we show that simply reading these persistent activations -- without any training -- yields competitive aggregate detection performance with strong adversarial robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：监狱攻击下的稳健有害特征：来自大型语言模型注意力头专业化的机制证据
监狱攻击绕过了大型语言模型的安全对齐，但其机制仍然不甚了解。我们提供证据表明，攻击并未全面消除安全特征，而是选择性地抑制特定的注意力头。我们识别出两种功能上不同的类型：集中在早期层的对抗性妥协头（ACHs），在攻击下被抑制；以及在中层的安全对齐头（SAHs），即使在攻击成功时也能保持稳健的激活。消融研究支持ACHs的因果作用以及SAHs对稳健激活的贡献：抑制少量ACHs足以在通常拒绝的输入上诱发类似监狱攻击的行为，而去除SAHs则显著削弱中层的安全激活。标记级归因进一步表明，ACH抑制是由攻击模板标记特定驱动的，提供了攻击为何能够通过ACH抑制绕过拒绝决策而保持SAHs支持的内部安全信号的机制性解释——这一现象我们称之为稳健有害特征。为了验证这种稳健性的实际意义，我们展示了仅仅读取这些持续的激活——无需任何训练——就能在强对抗稳健性下获得竞争性的整体检测性能。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the issue of jailbreak attacks that undermine the safety alignment of large language models (LLMs), a problem that has not been thoroughly understood in prior studies. Previous methods failed to identify the specific mechanisms through which these attacks operate, particularly the selective suppression of attention heads rather than a complete elimination of safety features. The proposed approach distinguishes between Adversarially Compromised Heads (ACHs) and Safety-Aligned Heads (SAHs), revealing that while ACHs are suppressed during attacks, SAHs maintain robust activations. This insight is well-motivated as it provides a mechanistic understanding of how attacks bypass safety measures. The paper contributes by demonstrating that suppressing a small number of ACHs can induce jailbreak-like behavior, while the removal of SAHs weakens safety activations. The methodology includes ablation studies and token-level attribution, leading to findings that simply monitoring these persistent activations can achieve competitive detection performance against jailbreak attacks, thus supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety.
本研究解决了越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLMs）安全对齐的挑战，而这些攻击的机制尚未得到充分理解。以往的方法未能有效识别这些攻击的运作方式，导致对安全特征的韧性理解存在空白。所提出的方法区分了两种类型的注意力头：在攻击中被抑制的对抗性受损头（ACHs）和保持激活的安全对齐头（SAHs）。这种区分使得对攻击如何绕过安全特征的机制有了更深入的理解，同时仍然保留了一些内部安全信号。本文的贡献在于证明抑制ACHs会导致类似越狱的行为，而SAHs的存在对维持安全激活至关重要。该方法包括消融研究和标记级归因，揭示了仅监测SAHs的持久激活即可实现对越狱攻击的竞争性检测性能，从而支持LLMs在实际应用中的韧性。
CASE-Bench: Context-Aware SafEty Benchmark for Large Language Models
Authors: Guangzhi Sun, Xiao Zhan, Shutong Feng, Philip C. Woodland, Jose Such
Venue: ICML 2025
First: 2025-01-24T21:55:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-28T22:17:10+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. This paper has been accepted at ICML 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human values is essential for their safe deployment and widespread adoption. Current LLM safety benchmarks often focus solely on the refusal of individual problematic queries, which overlooks the importance of the context where the query occurs and may cause undesired refusal of queries under safe contexts that diminish user experience. Addressing this gap, we introduce CASE-Bench, a Context-Aware SafEty Benchmark that integrates context into safety assessments of LLMs. CASE-Bench assigns distinct, formally described contexts to categorized queries based on Contextual Integrity theory. Additionally, in contrast to previous studies which mainly rely on majority voting from just a few annotators, we recruited a sufficient number of annotators necessary to ensure the detection of statistically significant differences among the experimental conditions based on power analysis. Our extensive analysis using CASE-Bench on various open-source and commercial LLMs reveals a substantial and significant influence of context on human judgments (p<0.0001 from a z-test), underscoring the necessity of context in safety evaluations. We also identify notable mismatches between human judgments and LLM responses, particularly in commercial models within safe contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CASE-Bench：面向上下文的安全基准测试用于大型语言模型
将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类价值观对齐对于其安全部署和广泛采用至关重要。目前的LLM安全基准测试通常仅关注个别问题查询的拒绝，忽视了查询发生的上下文的重要性，可能导致在安全上下文中不必要地拒绝查询，从而降低用户体验。为了解决这一问题，我们引入了CASE-Bench，一个将上下文整合到LLM安全评估中的面向上下文的安全基准测试。CASE-Bench根据上下文完整性理论为分类查询分配独特的、正式描述的上下文。此外，与以往主要依赖少数注释者的多数投票的研究不同，我们招募了足够数量的注释者，以确保根据功效分析检测实验条件之间的统计显著差异。我们对各种开源和商业LLM使用CASE-Bench进行的广泛分析揭示了上下文对人类判断的显著影响（p<0.0001，来自z检验），强调了上下文在安全评估中的必要性。我们还发现人类判断与LLM响应之间存在显著不匹配，特别是在安全上下文中的商业模型。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for aligning large language models (LLMs) with human values to ensure their safe deployment, highlighting the limitations of existing safety benchmarks that focus solely on individual problematic queries without considering the context. Previous methods often relied on majority voting from a limited number of annotators, which may not capture the nuances of context, leading to potential misjudgments in safety evaluations. The proposed CASE-Bench introduces a Context-Aware SafEty Benchmark that incorporates context into safety assessments based on Contextual Integrity theory, utilizing a sufficient number of annotators to detect statistically significant differences among experimental conditions. This methodology reveals a significant impact of context on human judgments regarding LLM safety, with findings indicating mismatches between human assessments and LLM responses, particularly in commercial models, thus contributing to a more nuanced understanding of safety in LLM deployment.
本研究关注于将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类价值观对齐的关键需求，以确保其安全部署，强调现有的安全基准往往忽视查询的上下文，导致不当拒绝，损害用户体验。以往的方法主要依赖于有限数量的注释者的多数投票，这可能无法捕捉上下文的细微差别，而提出的CASE-Bench则基于上下文完整性理论将上下文整合到安全评估中，并采用更多的注释者以增强统计可靠性。本文的贡献在于展示上下文对人类判断LLM安全性的显著影响，揭示了人类评估与LLM响应之间的差异，尤其是在商业模型中。该方法论涉及为分类查询分配不同的上下文，并在各种LLM上进行广泛分析，取得了统计显著的结果，支持了上下文在安全评估中的必要性，从而推动了LLM安全评估领域的发展。
SCARCE: Scalable Cascade Analysis for Rare-event Characterisation via Embeddings
Authors: Yingjie Wang, Yi Dong, Edmund Lau, Jie Meng, Taylor T Johnson, Xiaowei Huang
First: 2026-06-28T21:59:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-28T21:59:31+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 11 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rare events govern the safety profile of modern AI systems, yet their probabilities are extremely difficult to estimate: direct Monte Carlo requires prohibitive sample budgets. Subset Simulation (SS) addresses this by decomposing a rare-event probability into moderate conditional probabilities over nested intermediate events. However, classical SS requires a handcrafted scalar performance function whose sublevel sets define those events, demanding detailed knowledge of the failure geometry and limiting transfer to new domains. We propose SCARCE (Scalable Cascade Analysis for Rare-event Characterisation via Embeddings), which replaces the performance function with learned latent representations and geometric rulers that score proximity to failure regions. Adaptive thresholding constructs nested intermediate events directly from data. We formalise SCARCE through a non-negative supermartingale, yielding a high-probability upper envelope that remains valid under early stopping. On MNIST misclassification, where dense Monte Carlo provides ground truth, SCARCE achieves approximately 400--500 times lower mean absolute error than grid-searched traditional SS while eliminating systematic over-counting. We then study PAIR-style LLM jailbreaks under a fleet-level threat model with adversarial fraction $η$. On Llama-Guard-3-8B hidden states, a PCA-based ruler attains 2.6% mean relative error for $η\geq 10^{-3}$ against finite-sample references whose average bootstrap relative half-width is 27.9%, and transfers to a GCG-style corpus with 2.93% relative error after recalibration. A directional criterion $\mathrm{KL}(p_{\mathrm{good}}\,\|\,p_{\mathrm{bad}})$ ranks rulers consistently with estimation error (Spearman $ρ=0.83$).
中文标题/摘要
标题：SCARCE：通过嵌入进行稀有事件特征化的可扩展级联分析
稀有事件主导现代人工智能系统的安全特性，但其概率极难估计：直接的蒙特卡洛方法需要巨大的样本预算。子集模拟（SS）通过将稀有事件概率分解为嵌套中间事件的适度条件概率来解决这个问题。然而，经典的SS需要手工制作的标量性能函数，其子水平集定义这些事件，要求对失效几何形状有详细了解，并限制了向新领域的转移。我们提出SCARCE（通过嵌入进行稀有事件特征化的可扩展级联分析），用学习的潜在表示和几何尺代替性能函数，评分与失效区域的接近度。自适应阈值直接从数据构建嵌套中间事件。我们通过非负超鞅形式化SCARCE，产生一个在早期停止下仍然有效的高概率上包络。在MNIST错误分类中，稠密蒙特卡洛提供了真实值，SCARCE的平均绝对误差比网格搜索的传统SS低约400-500倍，同时消除了系统性过度计数。然后，我们在一个具有对抗性比例$η$的舰队级威胁模型下研究PAIR风格的LLM越狱。在Llama-Guard-3-8B隐藏状态上，基于PCA的尺在$η\geq 10^{-3}$时对有限样本参考的平均相对误差为2.6%，其平均自助法相对半宽度为27.9%，并在重新校准后转移到GCG风格的语料库，具有2.93%的相对误差。方向标准$\mathrm{KL}(p_{\mathrm{good}}\,\|\,p_{\mathrm{bad}})$与估计误差一致地对尺进行排名（斯皮尔曼$ρ=0.83$）。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of estimating rare event probabilities in AI systems, which is crucial for ensuring safety but is hindered by the limitations of traditional methods like Subset Simulation (SS) that require detailed knowledge of failure geometries. The proposed SCARCE method innovatively replaces the need for a handcrafted performance function with learned latent representations and geometric rulers, allowing for adaptive thresholding that directly constructs intermediate events from data. This approach effectively overcomes the limitations of classical SS, such as systematic over-counting and the need for extensive sample budgets. The methodology is formalized through a non-negative supermartingale, demonstrating significant improvements in performance; SCARCE achieves approximately 400-500 times lower mean absolute error on MNIST misclassification compared to traditional SS and shows promising results in estimating adversarial threats in LLM jailbreaks with low relative error, supporting its efficacy in practical applications.
本研究解决了在人工智能系统中估计稀有事件概率的挑战，这对于评估安全性至关重要，但使用传统方法（如蒙特卡洛模拟）由于样本需求高而难以估计。现有技术，特别是子集模拟（SS），依赖于手工制作的标量性能函数，这需要对失败几何形状有详细了解，限制了它们在新领域的适用性。提出的方法SCARCE创新性地用学习的潜在表示和几何尺代替这些性能函数，以评分与失败区域的接近度，从而允许自适应阈值直接从数据构建嵌套的中间事件。这种方法是合理的，因为它克服了经典SS的局限性，提供了一种可扩展的解决方案。该方法通过非负超马丁戈形式化SCARCE，在MNIST误分类等任务上实现了显著低于传统SS的平均绝对误差，并在分析PAIR风格的LLM越狱时表现出低相对误差，从而支持其增强稀有事件表征的目标。
The Joint Effect of Quantization and Sampling Temperature on LLM Safety Alignment: A Factorial Analysis
Authors: Hari Prasad, Ritam Pal
First: 2026-06-28T19:52:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-28T19:52:25+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 3 Figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern LLM deployments routinely compress models and raise sampling temperature to reduce cost, latency, or repetition, yet safety evaluations usually treat these choices as fixed implementation details. This leaves a practical uncertainty: does a model that is safe at FP16 and greedy decoding remain safe after it is quantized and sampled stochastically, or do the two deployment knobs amplify one another? We study this question with a factorial evaluation of 9 instruction-tuned models from six families, 3 precisions (FP16, GPTQ INT8, AWQ INT4), and 6 temperatures ($T{=}0$ to $1.0$), yielding 161 configurations and $\approx$322k responses judged by a six-model safety ensemble. Contrary to the concern that low-bit deployment broadly erodes alignment, standard non-adversarial quantization is usually safety-neutral: INT4 keeps or lowers attack success for 7 of 9 models, with clear degradation concentrated in the weakest baseline model, SmolLM3-3B ($18.5\%{\to}36.0\%$). The larger risk comes from sampling: higher temperature sharply increases decision instability for vulnerable models, with DFR reaching 53.0\% at $T{=}1.0$, even when average ASR changes modestly. Finally, the interaction is not a ``double penalty'': our Compound Degradation Index remains largely sub-additive ($-0.195$ to $+0.045$), indicating that quantization and temperature do not systematically compound. These results suggest a deployment rule of thumb: standard INT4/INT8 quantization can be reasonable for strongly aligned models, but safety claims at elevated temperature should report multi-sample stability, not only average attack success.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量化与采样温度对大型语言模型安全对齐的联合影响：一个因子分析
现代大型语言模型的部署通常会压缩模型并提高采样温度，以降低成本、延迟或重复性，但安全评估通常将这些选择视为固定的实施细节。这留下了一个实际的不确定性：在FP16和贪婪解码下安全的模型在量化和随机采样后是否仍然安全，或者这两个部署参数是否相互放大？我们通过对来自六个家族的9个指令调优模型、3种精度（FP16、GPTQ INT8、AWQ INT4）和6种温度（$T{=}0$到$1.0$）进行因子评估来研究这个问题，产生了161种配置和约322k个响应，由六个模型的安全集成进行评判。与低位部署普遍削弱对齐的担忧相反，标准的非对抗性量化通常是安全中性的：对于9个模型中的7个，INT4保持或降低攻击成功率，明显的降级集中在最弱的基线模型SmolLM3-3B（$18.5\%{\to}36.0\%$）。更大的风险来自采样：较高的温度显著增加了脆弱模型的决策不稳定性，在$T{=}1.0$时DFR达到53.0\%，即使平均ASR变化不大。最后，这种交互并不是“双重惩罚”：我们的复合降级指数在很大程度上保持亚加性（$-0.195$到$+0.045$），表明量化和温度并不会系统性地叠加。这些结果建议了一条部署经验法则：标准的INT4/INT8量化对于强对齐模型是合理的，但在高温下的安全声明应报告多样本稳定性，而不仅仅是平均攻击成功率。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the uncertainty surrounding the safety of large language models (LLMs) when subjected to quantization and varying sampling temperatures, which are common practices to optimize cost and performance. Previous methods typically treated these factors as fixed, failing to assess their combined effects on model safety. The proposed approach conducts a factorial analysis of 9 instruction-tuned models across different precisions and temperatures, revealing that while quantization generally maintains safety, higher sampling temperatures can significantly destabilize decision-making in vulnerable models. The paper contributes by establishing that standard quantization methods do not inherently compromise safety and emphasizes the need for evaluating multi-sample stability at elevated temperatures. The methodology involves evaluating 161 configurations and approximately 322,000 responses, demonstrating that INT4/INT8 quantization is acceptable for well-aligned models, but safety assessments must consider the variability introduced by sampling temperature.
本文探讨了在量化和不同采样温度下，大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性存在的实际不确定性，因为以往的评估通常将这些因素视为固定的。现有方法通常忽视量化与采样温度之间的相互作用，这可能导致误导性的安全评估。作者提出了一种因子分析方法，涉及9个指令调优模型，涵盖不同的精度和温度，共产生161种配置和约322,000个响应进行安全性评估。研究结果表明，标准的非对抗性量化通常对安全性中性，但较高的采样温度显著增加了脆弱模型的决策不稳定性。该研究为量化和温度之间的相互作用提供了细致的理解，建议对于良好对齐的模型，INT4/INT8量化是安全的，但强调在较高温度下需要报告多样本稳定性，以确保安全声明的有效性。
Sparse Autoencoders are Capable LLM Jailbreak Mitigators
Authors: Yannick Assogba, Jacopo Cortellazzi, Javier Abad, Pau Rodriguez, Xavier Suau, Arno Blaas
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-02-12T21:17:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-27T01:07:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the Mechanistic Interpretability Workshop, ICML 2026. 31 pages, 20 figures, 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks remain a persistent threat to large language model safety. We propose Context-Conditioned Delta Steering (CC-Delta), an SAE-based defense that identifies jailbreak-relevant sparse features by comparing token-level representations of the same harmful request with and without jailbreak context. Using paired harmful/jailbreak prompts, CC-Delta selects features via statistical testing and applies inference-time mean-shift steering in SAE latent space. Across four aligned instruction-tuned models and twelve jailbreak attacks, CC-Delta achieves comparable or better safety-utility tradeoffs than baseline defenses operating in dense latent space. In particular, our method clearly outperforms dense mean-shift steering on all four models, and particularly against out-of-distribution attacks, showing that steering in sparse SAE feature space offers advantages over steering in dense activation space for jailbreak mitigation. Our results suggest off-the-shelf SAEs trained for interpretability can be repurposed as practical jailbreak defenses without task-specific training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：稀疏自编码器能够缓解大型语言模型的越狱攻击
越狱攻击仍然是大型语言模型安全的持续威胁。我们提出了基于稀疏自编码器的上下文条件增量引导（CC-Delta）防御，通过比较同一有害请求在有无越狱上下文下的令牌级表示，识别与越狱相关的稀疏特征。使用成对的有害/越狱提示，CC-Delta通过统计测试选择特征，并在稀疏自编码器潜在空间中应用推理时均值偏移引导。在四个对齐的指令调优模型和十二个越狱攻击中，CC-Delta实现了与在稠密潜在空间中运行的基线防御相当或更好的安全效用权衡。特别是，我们的方法在所有四个模型上明显优于稠密均值偏移引导，尤其是在对抗分布外攻击时，表明在稀疏自编码器特征空间中的引导相较于在稠密激活空间中的引导在越狱缓解方面具有优势。我们的结果表明，经过可解释性训练的现成稀疏自编码器可以被重新用于作为实用的越狱防御，而无需特定任务的训练。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the ongoing threat of jailbreak attacks on large language models, which compromise their safety. Previous methods primarily utilized dense latent space for defense, leading to limitations in identifying and mitigating specific vulnerabilities associated with jailbreak contexts. The proposed Context-Conditioned Delta Steering (CC-Delta) approach leverages Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) to effectively identify relevant features by comparing token-level representations of harmful requests with and without jailbreak context, thus providing a more targeted defense mechanism. This paper contributes by demonstrating that off-the-shelf SAEs can be repurposed for jailbreak mitigation without requiring task-specific training. The methodology involves statistical testing to select features and applying mean-shift steering in the SAE latent space, achieving superior safety-utility tradeoffs across four instruction-tuned models against twelve jailbreak attacks, particularly excelling in out-of-distribution scenarios.

Just Ask: Curious Code Agents Reveal System Prompts in Frontier LLMs
Authors: Xiang Zheng, Yutao Wu, Hanxun Huang, Yige Li, Xingjun Ma, Bo Li, Yu-Gang Jiang, Cong Wang
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-01-29T03:53:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-26T10:38:52+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous code agents built on large language models are reshaping software and AI development through tool use, long-horizon reasoning, and self-directed interaction. However, this autonomy introduces a previously unrecognized security risk: agentic interaction fundamentally expands the LLM attack surface, enabling systematic probing and recovery of hidden system prompts that guide model behavior. We identify system prompt extraction as an emergent vulnerability intrinsic to code agents and present \textbf{\textsc{JustAsk}}, a self-evolving framework that autonomously discovers effective extraction strategies through interaction alone. Unlike prior prompt-engineering or dataset-based attacks, \textsc{JustAsk} requires no handcrafted prompts, labeled supervision, or privileged access beyond standard user interaction. It formulates extraction as an online exploration problem, using Upper Confidence Bound-based strategy selection and a hierarchical skill space spanning atomic probes and high-level orchestration. These skills exploit imperfect system-instruction generalization and inherent tensions between helpfulness and safety. Evaluated on \textbf{41} black-box commercial models across multiple providers, \textsc{JustAsk} consistently achieves full or near-complete system prompt recovery, revealing recurring design- and architecture-level vulnerabilities. Our results expose system prompts as a critical yet largely unprotected attack surface in modern agent systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：只需询问：好奇的代码代理揭示前沿大型语言模型中的系统提示
基于大型语言模型的自主代码代理通过工具使用、长远推理和自我导向交互正在重塑软件和人工智能开发。然而，这种自主性引入了一种之前未被认识的安全风险：代理交互从根本上扩展了大型语言模型的攻击面，使得系统提示的系统性探测和恢复成为可能，这些提示指导模型行为。我们将系统提示提取识别为代码代理内在的一个新兴漏洞，并提出\textbf{\textsc{JustAsk}}，一个通过交互自主发现有效提取策略的自我演化框架。与之前的提示工程或基于数据集的攻击不同，\textsc{JustAsk}不需要手工提示、标记监督或超出标准用户交互的特权访问。它将提取形式化为一个在线探索问题，使用基于上置信界的策略选择和跨越原子探测和高级编排的层次技能空间。这些技能利用了系统指令泛化的不完美性以及有用性与安全性之间的内在张力。在对\textbf{41}个来自多个提供商的黑箱商业模型进行评估时，\textsc{JustAsk}始终实现了完整或近乎完整的系统提示恢复，揭示了反复出现的设计和架构级漏洞。我们的结果揭示了系统提示作为现代代理系统中一个关键但大多未受保护的攻击面。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the emerging security risks posed by autonomous code agents built on large language models (LLMs), specifically the vulnerability of system prompt extraction that can be exploited through agentic interactions. Previous methods relied on prompt-engineering or dataset-based attacks, which required handcrafted prompts and labeled supervision, limiting their effectiveness and applicability. The proposed approach, JustAsk, autonomously discovers effective extraction strategies through interaction alone, framing the problem as an online exploration task that utilizes Upper Confidence Bound-based strategy selection. This method is well-motivated as it addresses the inherent tensions between helpfulness and safety in LLMs. The contribution of the paper lies in demonstrating that JustAsk can achieve full or near-complete recovery of system prompts across 41 black-box commercial models, revealing significant vulnerabilities in their design and architecture, thus highlighting system prompts as a critical attack surface in modern agent systems.

How Reliable Is Your Jailbreak Judge? Calibration and Adversarial Robustness of Automated ASR Scoring
Authors: Yang Gao
First: 2026-06-24T07:14:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-25T02:04:55+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures, 2 tables, Code: github.com/gy15901580825/judgeflip
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Almost every paper on LLM jailbreaks and prompt injection reports an attack-success rate (ASR), and that number is assigned not by people but by an automated judge: either a safety classifier trained for the task, or a general chat model prompted to grade. The judge is rarely checked. We check it. Using 596 human-labeled completions from the HarmBench classifier validation set, we compare the two judge families against human majority votes and then attack them. The two families fail in opposite ways. The dedicated classifier over-flags (precision 0.835, recall 0.974); three different LLM-as-judges keep high precision (0.81 to 0.94) but show erratic recall (0.06 to 0.65), so the same responses produce very different ASR depending on which judge scores them. The two families also differ sharply in robustness. Wrappers that leave the harmful text untouched and only add benign framing flip every LLM-judge between 57% and 100% of the time, and a single prepended refusal sentence accounts for much of this (39% to 88%). The dedicated classifier resists these surface attacks (at most 6.7%), but a white-box GCG attack on its open weights flips 70% of confident true positives (21 of 30; 95% CI 54 to 86%) even at a small optimization budget. A two-annotator audit confirms the attacks leave the harm intact: every one of 80 sampled flips still contained the harmful content. Because a large and growing share of reported ASR comes from LLM-judges, many such numbers are unreliable both on average and under deliberate pressure. We recommend that papers report judge precision and recall on a human-labeled slice, report ASR corrected for judge precision, and include an adversarial check of the judge. Our code is released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：你的越狱评估器有多可靠？自动化ASR评分的校准与对抗鲁棒性
几乎每篇关于LLM越狱和提示注入的论文都报告了攻击成功率（ASR），而这个数字不是由人类赋予的，而是由一个自动评估器给出的：要么是为此任务训练的安全分类器，要么是被提示进行评分的一般聊天模型。评估器很少被检查。我们进行了检查。使用来自HarmBench分类器验证集的596个人工标注的完成结果，我们将这两类评估器与人类多数投票进行比较，然后对其进行攻击。这两类评估器在失败方式上截然相反。专用分类器过度标记（精确度0.835，召回率0.974）；三种不同的LLM作为评估者保持高精度（0.81到0.94），但显示出不稳定的召回率（0.06到0.65），因此相同的响应根据哪个评估器评分会产生非常不同的ASR。这两类评估器在鲁棒性上也有显著差异。那些不改变有害文本，仅添加良性框架的包装器使每个LLM评估者在57%到100%之间翻转，而一个单独的前置拒绝句子占据了其中很大一部分（39%到88%）。专用分类器抵御这些表面攻击（最多6.7%），但对其开放权重的白盒GCG攻击在小的优化预算下翻转了70%的自信真阳性（30个中的21个；95% CI 54到86%）。两个标注者的审计确认攻击保持了有害内容的完整性：80个抽样翻转中的每一个仍然包含有害内容。由于越来越多的报告ASR来自LLM评估者，许多这样的数字在平均值和故意压力下都是不可靠的。我们建议论文报告人类标注切片上的评估器精度和召回率，报告经过评估器精度修正的ASR，并包括对评估器的对抗检查。我们的代码已发布。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the reliability of automated judges used to report attack-success rates (ASR) in studies on LLM jailbreaks and prompt injections, highlighting that these judges are often unverified. Previous methods relied on either dedicated safety classifiers or general chat models, which exhibited significant shortcomings in precision and recall. RAS: Measuring LLM Safety Through Refusal Alignment
Authors: Chang-Chieh Huang, Yan-Lun Chen, Chia-Mu Yu, Wei-Bin Lee
First: 2026-06-24T12:19:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-24T12:19:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) is commonly performed by querying models with unsafe or jailbreak prompts and judging whether their outputs violate a safety policy. Although useful, output-level evaluation is expensive, sensitive to judge choice, and easily tied to fixed question banks. We propose **SafeVec**, a white-box evaluation procedure that measures safety from internal representations rather than generated answers. **SafeVec** first extracts layer-wise refusal directions from a safety-aligned reference model, then selects stable layer windows where safe and unsafe behaviors are separable, and finally scores a target model by measuring whether its hidden states align with these refusal directions under unsafe and jailbreak prompts. The resulting metric, **RAS** (**R**efusal **A**lignment **S**core), maps representation-level refusal alignment to a calibrated 0-100 safety score. Across `Llama`, `Gemma`, and `Qwen` model families, RAS separates aligned models from uncensored and abliterated variants, tracks output-level attack success rate, and is substantially faster than judge-based evaluation. These results suggest that refusal alignment provides a compact and efficient signal for white-box LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RAS：通过拒绝对齐测量大型语言模型的安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全性评估通常通过使用不安全或越狱提示查询模型，并判断其输出是否违反安全政策。尽管有用，输出级评估成本高、对评判者选择敏感，并且容易与固定问题库挂钩。我们提出了**SafeVec**，一种白盒评估程序，从内部表示而非生成答案来测量安全性。**SafeVec**首先从安全对齐的参考模型中提取逐层拒绝方向，然后选择安全和不安全行为可分离的稳定层窗口，最后通过测量目标模型的隐藏状态在不安全和越狱提示下是否与这些拒绝方向对齐来评分。最终指标**RAS**（**R**efusal **A**lignment **S**core）将表示级拒绝对齐映射到校准的0-100安全分数。在`Llama`、`Gemma`和`Qwen`模型系列中，RAS将对齐模型与未审查和被消除的变体区分开，跟踪输出级攻击成功率，并且比基于评判者的评估快得多。这些结果表明，拒绝对齐为白盒LLM安全评估提供了紧凑而高效的信号。

The research addresses the challenge of evaluating the safety of large language models (LLMs), which has traditionally relied on output-level assessments that are costly, subjective, and dependent on fixed question banks. Existing methods often struggle with these limitations, prompting the authors to propose a novel approach called SafeVec, which evaluates safety based on internal representations rather than outputs. FinRED: An Expert-Guided Benchmark Generation and Evaluation Framework for Financial LLM Red-Teaming
Authors: Chaeyun Kim, Daeyoung Park, Junghwan Kim, Jinyoung Jeong, Eunji Song, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
First: 2026-06-18T07:46:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-24T07:42:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing safety benchmarks target general adversarial scenarios but miss finance-specific risks. Financial LLMs face regulatory compliance violations, fraud facilitation, and systemic trust erosion that require targeted evaluation. We introduce FinRED, an expert-guided red-teaming framework for financial LLM safety evaluation developed with financial experts. FinRED uses a novel two-level taxonomy mapping global standards (e.g., FATF and EU DORA) to threats ranging from regulatory evasion to complex fraud, integrated with a scalable pipeline that converts real financial documents into context-rich red-teaming Behavioral Prompts (seeds) through an expert-defined schema. Rigorous expert validation confirms seed plausibility and realism for meaningful LLM safety evaluation. We also provide an expert-validated, finance-specific rubric that goes beyond disclaimer checks, aligns more closely with human experts than static one-size-fits-all rubrics, and reduces critical false negatives from 28 to 12. Aligned with internationally adopted risk-management and information-security standards (e.g., ISO/IEC 27001), FinRED is deployed in South Korea's Financial Security Institute (FSI) regulatory sandbox for generative AI security evaluation in real financial services. To mitigate dual-use risks, the dataset, generation pipeline, prompt template, and evaluation framework are gated for qualified researchers at https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper and https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FinRED：一个专家指导的金融LLM红队评估基准生成框架
现有的安全基准针对一般对抗场景，但忽视了金融特定风险。金融LLM面临合规违规、欺诈促进和系统信任侵蚀等问题，需要针对性评估。我们推出了FinRED，这是一个由金融专家开发的专家指导的红队框架，用于金融LLM安全评估。FinRED使用一种新颖的两级分类法，将全球标准（如FATF和EU DORA）映射到从合规规避到复杂欺诈的威胁，结合一个可扩展的管道，通过专家定义的模式将真实金融文档转换为上下文丰富的红队行为提示（种子）。严格的专家验证确认种子的合理性和真实性，以便进行有意义的LLM安全评估。我们还提供了一个经过专家验证的金融特定评分标准，超越了免责声明检查，更加贴近人类专家，而不是静态的一刀切评分标准，并将关键假阴性从28减少到12。FinRED与国际公认的风险管理和信息安全标准（如ISO/IEC 27001）保持一致，已在韩国金融安全研究所（FSI）的监管沙箱中部署，用于真实金融服务中的生成AI安全评估。为了减轻双重用途风险，数据集、生成管道、提示模板和评估框架对合格研究人员进行了限制，网址为https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper和https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacies of existing safety benchmarks for financial language models (LLMs), which primarily focus on general adversarial scenarios and overlook finance-specific risks such as regulatory compliance violations and fraud. Previous methods fail to provide targeted evaluations, leading to critical false negatives in safety assessments. The proposed FinRED framework, developed with input from financial experts, introduces a two-level taxonomy that aligns global standards with specific financial threats and utilizes a scalable pipeline to create context-rich red-teaming Behavioral Prompts from real financial documents. This approach not only enhances the realism and plausibility of evaluation seeds but also incorporates an expert-validated rubric that significantly reduces false negatives. FinRED has been implemented in South Korea's Financial Security Institute regulatory sandbox, demonstrating its effectiveness in evaluating generative AI security in financial services, thereby supporting its goal of improving safety assessments in finance.
本研究解决了现有金融大型语言模型（LLM）安全基准不足的问题，现有基准通常关注一般对抗场景，而忽视了金融特有的风险，如合规违规和欺诈。以往的方法缺乏针对性，导致安全评估存在显著缺口。提出的FinRED框架与金融专家共同开发，采用两级分类法，将全球标准映射到特定金融威胁，并利用可扩展的管道从真实金融文档中创建上下文丰富的红队行为提示。该方法经过专家验证，确保提示的现实性和可信度，最终形成了一个金融特定的评分标准，显著减少了关键的漏报。FinRED已在韩国金融安全研究所的监管沙箱中实施，证明其在金融服务中评估生成性人工智能安全的有效性，从而支持其在该领域增强安全评估的目标。
TROPT: An Open Framework for Unifying and Advancing Discrete Text Optimization
Authors: Matan Ben-Tov, Mahmood Sharif
First: 2026-06-22T15:44:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-22T15:44:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Discrete text-trigger optimization -- searching for text sequences that, when ingested by a model, steer it toward a specified objective -- underpins model red-teaming (e.g., LLM jailbreaks), as well as auditing and interpretability. However, the current state of discrete optimizers hinders their adoption and progress. First, existing optimizers, when open-sourced at all, are scattered across research codebases tied to specific models, objectives, and problem domains. Second, optimizer variants proliferate, each requiring engineering overhead to use or extend, and remaining hard to compare head-to-head. Together, these raise the bar for adopting optimizers in existing or new domains, and for advancing them via new strategies. We address these gaps with TROPT, the first open-source framework that unifies discrete optimizers' execution and standardizes their development under a single interface. TROPT makes it easy to customize end-to-end optimization recipes by swapping any component -- models, objectives, and optimizers -- extending its reach across domains and new applications. TROPT currently ships with 30+ optimization recipes -- covering applications such as jailbreaking and probing model internals -- built from 15+ optimizers (spanning white-box to black-box access) and 15+ losses, from foundational to state-of-the-art methods. Demonstrating its utility, we leverage TROPT in several studies: (i) controlled, large-scale experiments comparing and enhancing optimization strategies for LLM jailbreaks, revealing potent-yet-underadopted techniques; and (ii) porting optimizers from one domain (e.g., LLM jailbreak) to new domains (e.g., corpus-poisoning embedding model). In all, TROPT significantly lowers the barrier to adopting and advancing discrete text optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TROPT：一个统一和推进离散文本优化的开放框架
离散文本触发优化——寻找文本序列，当被模型摄取时，引导其朝向特定目标——是模型红队（例如，LLM越狱）以及审计和可解释性的基础。然而，当前离散优化器的状态阻碍了它们的采用和进展。首先，现有的优化器，即使开源，也分散在与特定模型、目标和问题领域相关的研究代码库中。其次，优化器变体层出不穷，每个都需要工程开销来使用或扩展，并且难以进行直接比较。这些因素共同提高了在现有或新领域中采用优化器的门槛，并通过新策略推进它们。我们通过TROPT解决这些问题，这是第一个统一离散优化器执行并在单一接口下标准化其开发的开源框架。TROPT使得通过更换任何组件——模型、目标和优化器——轻松定制端到端优化配方，扩展其在不同领域和新应用中的适用性。TROPT目前提供30多个优化配方——涵盖越狱和探测模型内部等应用——构建于15个以上的优化器（从白盒到黑盒访问）和15个以上的损失函数，从基础方法到最先进的方法。为了展示其效用，我们在几项研究中利用TROPT：（i）控制的大规模实验比较和增强LLM越狱的优化策略，揭示出强大但未被广泛采用的技术；（ii）将优化器从一个领域（例如，LLM越狱）移植到新领域（例如，语料库中毒嵌入模型）。总之，TROPT显著降低了采用和推进离散文本优化的门槛。

Culturally-Adapted Red-Teaming Across East and Southeast Asian Contexts: A Methodological and Comparative Analysis
Authors: Hyeji Choi, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-06-08T08:17:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-22T07:46:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICML 2026 Workshop on Culture X AI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multilingual safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) has predominantly relied on direct translation (DT) of English benchmarks into target languages - an approach that converts surface-level linguistic form while failing to reflect the cultural context embedded in threat scenarios, social norms, and legal frameworks. We construct paired DT and culturally-adapted (CA) datasets via 1:1 seed matching for four languages - Korean (KO), Japanese (JA), Thai (TH), and Khmer (KM) - and compare Attack Success Rate (ASR) and Cultural Realism scores across four open-source LLM. CA prompts yield Delta-ASR > 0 across all 16 language x model combinations (mean +9.3 pp), and DT-based evaluation underestimates risk in 44 of 48 category x language combinations. Language-level analysis reveals that the distribution of threat forms is heterogeneous across languages. Cultural Realism analysis further shows that DT Cultural Depth (C3) scores remain consistently below 1.0 out of 3.0 across all four languages (mean 0.17), whereas CA scores reach up to 2.51, indicating that direct translation produces inputs systematically divergent from those encountered in real-world multicultural settings. These findings demonstrate that adapting benchmarks to language-specific cultural contexts - rather than relying on linguistic translation alone - is necessary for valid multilingual LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：跨东亚和东南亚背景的文化适应性红队：方法论和比较分析
大型语言模型（LLMs）的多语言安全评估主要依赖于将英语基准直接翻译（DT）为目标语言，这种方法仅转换表层语言形式，未能反映威胁场景、社会规范和法律框架中嵌入的文化背景。我们通过1:1种子匹配构建了四种语言（韩语、日语、泰语和高棉语）的配对DT和文化适应（CA）数据集，并比较了四个开源LLM的攻击成功率（ASR）和文化现实评分。CA提示在所有16种语言x模型组合中均产生Delta-ASR > 0（平均+9.3个百分点），而基于DT的评估在48个类别x语言组合中低估了风险。语言级分析显示，威胁形式的分布在不同语言中是异质的。文化现实分析进一步表明，DT文化深度（C3）评分在所有四种语言中始终低于3.0的1.0（平均0.17），而CA评分最高可达2.51，表明直接翻译产生的输入与现实世界多文化环境中遇到的输入系统性地不同。这些发现表明，适应特定语言文化背景的基准，而不仅仅依赖语言翻译，对于有效的多语言LLM安全评估是必要的。

Previous methods have overlooked the nuances of cultural norms and legal frameworks, leading to an underestimation of risks in non-English contexts. AgentLens: Interpretable Safety Steering via Mechanistic Subspaces for Multi-Turn Coding Agent
Authors: Weidi Luo, Qiming Zhang, Yihao Quan, Mingyu Jin, Jie Cai, Chaowei Xiao, Jingcheng Niu, Zhen Xiang
First: 2026-06-21T21:13:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-21T21:13:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Coding agents based on large language models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable autonomous capabilities, but they also introduce significant safety and misuse risks during multi-turn interactions with external environments. Existing safety mechanisms mainly rely on external guardrails, which have a limited ability to perform fine-grained behavioral control during execution. Meanwhile, recent mechanistic interpretability methods for LLM safety are mostly confined to single-turn or jailbreak-style QA settings, limiting their ability to capture the evolving risk dynamics of multi-turn agent execution. In this paper, we investigate the safety of multi-turn coding agents from an internal perspective. We propose AgentLens (Mechanistic Subspace Intervention and Steering), a white-box defense framework that performs runtime safety detection and representation-level mitigation for coding agents. Unlike conventional agent guardrails, AgentLens detect harmful execution states from step-level hidden representations and mitigate unsafe behavior by intervening in a 10-dimensional subspace within a single layer. To support this research, we introduce the Mechanistic Agent Safety (MAS) benchmark, comprising comprehensively annotated multi-turn execution trajectories across 194 tasks using LLaMA-3.1-8B, Qwen-2.5-7B, and Gemma-2-9B. Extensive experiments show that AgentLens achieves strong safety detection performance, provides preliminary evidence for lookahead risk anticipation, and substantially reduces harmful actions of the coding agent, establishing a foundation for applying mechanistic interpretability to dynamic LLM agent safety. The code is available at: https://github.com/EddyLuo1232/AgentLens
中文标题/摘要

基于大型语言模型（LLMs）的编码代理展示了显著的自主能力，但在与外部环境的多轮交互中也引入了重大安全和误用风险。现有的安全机制主要依赖外部护栏，在执行过程中对细粒度行为控制的能力有限。同时，最近的LLM安全机制可解释性方法大多局限于单轮或越狱式问答设置，限制了其捕捉多轮代理执行中不断变化的风险动态的能力。本文从内部视角研究多轮编码代理的安全性。我们提出了AgentLens（机制子空间干预与引导），这是一个白盒防御框架，能够对编码代理进行运行时安全检测和表示级别的缓解。与传统的代理护栏不同，AgentLens通过从步骤级隐藏表示中检测有害执行状态，并通过干预单层内的10维子空间来缓解不安全行为。为了支持这项研究，我们引入了机制代理安全（MAS）基准，涵盖了使用LLaMA-3.1-8B、Qwen-2.5-7B和Gemma-2-9B的194个任务的全面注释的多轮执行轨迹。大量实验表明，AgentLens实现了强大的安全检测性能，为前瞻性风险预判提供了初步证据，并显著减少了编码代理的有害行为，为将机制可解释性应用于动态LLM代理安全奠定了基础。代码可在：https://github.com/EddyLuo1232/AgentLens

Previous methods primarily focus on single-turn interactions or jailbreak-style question-answering, failing to capture the evolving risk dynamics in multi-turn scenarios. SPHINX: First Explain, Then Explore
Authors: Nguyen Do, Tue M. Cao, Tien Van Do, András Hajdu, Tamás Bérczes, My T. Thai
First: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00
Comments: 13 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generating adversarial driving scenarios is critical for evaluating and improving autonomous vehicle decision-making systems in simulation. Recent approaches, such as ChatScene and LLM-Attacker, rely primarily on the prior knowledge of Large Language Models and Vision-Language Models to generate driving scenarios procedurally. We argue that adversarial scenes should be generated based on the failure diagnosis (e.g., indecisiveness, multi-frame inconsistency) of the driving policy to specifically address the policy's weaknesses instead of relying on prior assumptions. In this paper, we propose SPHINX, a closed-loop framework for adversarial scenario synthesis guided by a simple principle: first explain, then explore. Beyond blindly exploring the scenario space, SPHINX leverages explainable artificial intelligence methods to analyze the policy, identifying key visual concepts and their influence on policy outputs, and the uncertainty of the decisions. Given the interpretable evidence extracted from the policy's own decision process, we use a vision language model to rationalize and criticize failure modes of the current policy. These critics are then used to generate targeted adversarial scenarios for policy retraining and improvement. We demonstrate that SPHINX can highlight an interpretable account of policy failures while other adversarial scene generation cannot. Across the evaluated benchmarks and test suites, SPHINX can be applied to diverse state-of-the-art autonomous vehicle architectures and yields consistent robustness improvements over existing scenario-generation methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPHINX：先解释，再探索
生成对抗驾驶场景对于评估和改进自主车辆决策系统在仿真中的表现至关重要。最近的方法，如ChatScene和LLM-Attacker，主要依赖于大型语言模型和视觉-语言模型的先验知识来程序性地生成驾驶场景。我们认为，对抗场景应基于驾驶策略的失败诊断（例如，优柔寡断、多帧不一致）生成，以具体解决策略的弱点，而不是依赖于先验假设。本文提出了SPHINX，一个闭环框架，用于对抗场景合成，其指导原则是：先解释，再探索。SPHINX不仅仅是盲目探索场景空间，而是利用可解释人工智能方法分析策略，识别关键视觉概念及其对策略输出的影响，以及决策的不确定性。根据从策略自身决策过程中提取的可解释证据，我们使用视觉语言模型来合理化和批评当前策略的失败模式。这些批评随后用于生成针对性的对抗场景，以进行策略再训练和改进。我们证明SPHINX能够突出政策失败的可解释性，而其他对抗场景生成方法则无法做到。在评估的基准和测试套件中，SPHINX可以应用于多种最先进的自主车辆架构，并在现有场景生成方法上实现一致的鲁棒性提升。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the need for effective generation of adversarial driving scenarios to enhance the evaluation of autonomous vehicle decision-making systems. The proposed SPHINX framework differs by utilizing a closed-loop approach that first explains the failures of the driving policy and then explores the scenario space based on these insights. This method is well-motivated as it focuses on diagnosing failures like indecisiveness and multi-frame inconsistency, leading to the generation of targeted adversarial scenarios for policy improvement. The contribution of the paper lies in demonstrating that SPHINX provides interpretable insights into policy failures and achieves consistent robustness improvements across various benchmarks and state-of-the-art autonomous vehicle architectures compared to existing methods.

Enhancing LLM Safety Through a Theoretical Minimax Game Lens
Authors: Yihe Deng, Yu Yang, Junkai Zhang, Wei Wang, Bo Li
First: 2025-02-07T18:45:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-15T02:50:15+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 9 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) necessitates effective mechanisms to ensure their responsible deployment by accurately distinguishing unsafe content from benign content. While substantial safety datasets are available in English, multilingual safety modeling remains underexplored due to limited open-source safety datasets in other languages. Even within English datasets, safe yet sensitive corner-case content is scarce, leading to shortcut learning by models and non-trivial false-positive rates. To mitigate these issues, we introduce a novel minimax reinforcement learning (RL) framework wherein a data generator and a classifier model co-evolve, facilitating the production of high-quality synthetic multilingual safety data. We theoretically formalize this interaction as a minimax game and rigorously demonstrate convergence to a Nash equilibrium. Empirical evaluations confirm that our synthetic data generation method significantly enhances the classifier model performance, enabling a substantially smaller model to surpass the state-of-the-art by nearly 10% on English benchmarks while achieving 4.5x faster inference speed. These results establish a scalable and efficient methodology for synthetic data generation, advancing the development of safer and more robust multilingual LLM deployments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过理论最小最大博弈视角增强大型语言模型安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展需要有效机制，以确保其负责任的部署，准确区分不安全内容与良性内容。虽然英语中有大量安全数据集，但由于其他语言中开放源代码安全数据集有限，多语言安全建模仍未得到充分探索。即使在英语数据集中，安全但敏感的边缘案例内容也很稀缺，导致模型的捷径学习和非平凡的误报率。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了一种新颖的最小最大强化学习（RL）框架，其中数据生成器和分类模型共同进化，促进高质量合成多语言安全数据的生成。我们将这种交互理论化为最小最大博弈，并严格证明其收敛到纳什均衡。实证评估确认，我们的合成数据生成方法显著提升了分类模型的性能，使得一个显著更小的模型在英语基准测试中超越了最先进的技术近10%，同时实现了4.5倍的推理速度提升。这些结果建立了一种可扩展且高效的合成数据生成方法，推动了更安全、更强大的多语言LLM部署的发展。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the urgent need for effective safety mechanisms in large language models (LLMs) due to their rapid advancement and the challenges in distinguishing unsafe from benign content, particularly in multilingual contexts where safety datasets are limited. Previous methods have struggled with the scarcity of safe yet sensitive content, leading to shortcut learning and high false-positive rates. The proposed approach introduces a minimax reinforcement learning framework that allows a data generator and classifier to co-evolve, producing high-quality synthetic multilingual safety data and theoretically formalizing this interaction as a minimax game. This methodology contributes to the field by significantly improving classifier performance, with empirical results showing a nearly 10% improvement over state-of-the-art models on English benchmarks and a 4.5x increase in inference speed, thus supporting the goal of developing safer multilingual LLMs.
本研究解决了由于大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展而迫切需要有效安全机制的问题，尤其是在多语言环境中，区分不安全内容和良性内容的挑战更为突出，因为安全数据集的数量有限。以往的方法主要依赖现有的英语数据集，这些数据集往往缺乏多样化和敏感的边缘案例，导致模型的捷径学习和较高的误报率。所提出的方法引入了一种极小极大强化学习框架，使数据生成器和分类器能够共同演化，生成高质量的多语言安全数据，并将这一过程理论化为极小极大博弈。这种方法不仅提升了分类器模型的性能，还显示出显著的改进，较小的模型在英语基准测试中超越了现有技术近10%，并实现了4.5倍的推理速度，从而为更安全和更强大的多语言LLM部署的发展做出了贡献。
GAS-Leak-LLM: Genetic Algorithm-Based Suffix Optimization for Black-Box LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Aman Anifer, Vignesh Kumar Kembu, Vishnu M, Antonino Nocera, Vinod P., Amal Murali PK, Akshay S Rajan
First: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) constitute pivotal components within the AI-dominated information technology ecosystem. To mitigate risks associated with harmful or policy-violating outputs, commercial systems employ advanced alignment strategies and multi-layered content moderation mechanisms. Despite these safeguards, recent research has demonstrated that LLMs remain vulnerable to adversarial manipulation, particularly through jailbreaking and prompt injection techniques. In this work, we propose GAS-Leak-LLM a novel jailbreaking attack based on a genetic algorithm that systematically evolves adversarial suffix to bypass safety constraints. Operating in a strict black-box setting, our method requires no access to model parameters or internals, thereby reflecting realistic threat scenarios in deployed systems. Through the iterative application of selection, mutation, and crossover heuristics, the framework systematically explores the discrete prompt space to identify high-fitness adversarial suffixes. Empirical findings reveal critical shortcomings in existing safety enforcement mechanisms and confirm the effectiveness and practical viability of the proposed attack.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GAS-Leak-LLM：基于遗传算法的黑箱LLM越狱后缀优化
大型语言模型（LLMs）是AI主导的信息技术生态系统中的关键组成部分。为了减轻与有害或违反政策输出相关的风险，商业系统采用先进的对齐策略和多层次内容审核机制。尽管有这些保护措施，最近的研究表明，LLMs仍然容易受到对抗性操控，特别是通过越狱和提示注入技术。在本研究中，我们提出了GAS-Leak-LLM，一种基于遗传算法的新型越狱攻击，系统地演化对抗性后缀以绕过安全约束。在严格的黑箱环境中，我们的方法不需要访问模型参数或内部结构，从而反映了已部署系统中的现实威胁场景。通过选择、突变和交叉启发式的迭代应用，该框架系统地探索离散提示空间，以识别高适应性的对抗性后缀。实证研究揭示了现有安全执行机制的关键缺陷，并确认了所提攻击的有效性和实际可行性。

CHILLGuard: Towards Fine-Grained Chinese LLM Safety Guardrail with Scalable Data Construction and Model-aware Preference Alignment
Authors: Wenbo Yu, Bohua Wang, Hao Fang, Kuofeng Gao, Jingru Zeng, Xiaochen Yang, Tianyi Zhang, Xiaoxiao Ma, Jiawei Kong, Hao Wu, Bin Chen, Shu-Tao Xia, Min Zhang
First: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Malicious content generated from large language models (LLMs) could pose severe safety risks and ethical concerns. While existing LLM safety guardrails excel in English or multilingual settings, they lack adaptation to Chinese-specific regulatory policies, cultural context and linguistic nuances, failing to support fine-grained risk classification for diverse deployment needs. In this paper, we introduce a 5-macro, 31-micro category fine-grained risk taxonomy for Chinese scenarios, and build CHILLGuard: a dedicated Chinese LLM content safety guardrail. To address the critical scarcity of high-quality annotated Chinese safety data, we propose a scalable multi-stage data construction pipeline: we expand multi-source corpus via retrieval-augmented generation, generate implicit harmful samples through prompt engineering rewriting, and refine high-quality data via multi-model voting-based label calibration. Based on this, we build CHILLGuardTrain, a large-scale training set with 405,007 samples, and CHILLGuardTest, a rigorously curated annotated test set with 51,745 samples. We then train CHILLGuard on CHILLGuardTrain under a generator-classifier collaborative framework via Model-aware Direct Preference Optimization. Extensive experiments under multiple settings demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of CHILLGuard, e.g., a 15.92% improvement of F1 score over Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict on our benchmark. We will release our resources at https://github.com/cswbyu/CHILLGuard.

Do You Really Need a GPU to Guard Your LLM? CPU-Class Classifiers and Multi-Stage Pipelines for Safety Enforcement at Scale
Authors: Vasudev Majhi, Dhruv Gupta, Advait Singh, Matthew Barker, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2025-12-22T04:00:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T05:46:54+00:00
Comments: Under Review. 25 pages, 5 figures, 38 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety classifiers that screen LLM inputs for jailbreak attempts have become standard deployment components, yet almost all production systems rely on GPU-based models: fine-tuned transformers and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines. These approaches impose significant per-query latency and infrastructure cost. Very little research has asked whether CPU-based classifiers, such as support vector machines and gradient-boosted trees trained on TF-IDF features, can match their accuracy across the conditions that production deployments encounter. We evaluate five CPU classifier families, Mamba-130M as an SSM-based GPU classifier, and transformer-based GPU models (DeBERTa-v3 and Gemma-2B with LoRA) across nine jailbreak sources and three regimes: in-distribution (D1), out-of-distribution (D2), and adversarially obfuscated (D3). On D1, the best CPU classifier matches the best transformer GPU model at roughly one-fifth the deployment cost. On D2, CPU classifiers fail via confident miscalibration, producing high-confidence false negatives that bypass escalation entirely. On D3, CPU classifiers outperform transformer GPU models by more than 26 percentage points in F1. Based on these complementary failure modes, we design GuardChain, a three-stage safety pipeline (Regex -> CPU -> GPU) that routes each prompt to the cheapest stage capable of a confident decision. The CPU stage alone resolves 80\% of in-distribution prompts at near-peak accuracy, and the GPU stage recovers the out-of-distribution failures. For practitioners deploying LLM safety at scale, this work provides evidence that GPU-class infrastructure is unnecessary for the majority of traffic.
中文标题/摘要
标题：您真的需要 GPU 来保护您的 LLM 吗？用于安全执行的 CPU 类分类器和多阶段管道
用于筛查 LLM 输入以防止越狱尝试的安全分类器已成为标准部署组件，但几乎所有生产系统都依赖于基于 GPU 的模型：微调的变换器和 LLM 作为裁判的管道。这些方法在每个查询上都带来了显著的延迟和基础设施成本。很少有研究探讨基于 CPU 的分类器，如支持向量机和基于 TF-IDF 特征训练的梯度提升树，是否能在生产部署所遇到的条件下匹配其准确性。 我们评估了五种 CPU 分类器系列，Mamba-130M 作为基于 SSM 的 GPU 分类器，以及基于变换器的 GPU 模型（DeBERTa-v3 和 Gemma-2B 与 LoRA）在九个越狱来源和三个模式下的表现：分布内（D1）、分布外（D2）和对抗性混淆（D3）。在 D1 上，最佳 CPU 分类器的表现与最佳变换器 GPU 模型相当，部署成本约为其五分之一。在 D2 上，CPU 分类器因自信的错误校准而失败，产生高置信度的假阴性，完全绕过升级。在 D3 上，CPU 分类器在 F1 上的表现超过变换器 GPU 模型超过 26 个百分点。 基于这些互补的失败模式，我们设计了 GuardChain，一个三阶段安全管道（Regex -> CPU -> GPU），将每个提示路由到能够做出自信决策的最便宜阶段。仅 CPU 阶段就以接近峰值的准确率解决了 80% 的分布内提示，而 GPU 阶段则恢复了分布外的失败。对于大规模部署 LLM 安全的从业者而言，这项工作提供了证据，表明 GPU 类基础设施对于大多数流量来说并非必要。

NeST: Neuron Selective Tuning for LLM Safety
Authors: Sasha Behrouzi, Lichao Wu, Mohamadreza Rostami, Ahmad-Reza Sadeghi
First: 2026-02-18T20:01:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-12T11:06:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment is essential for the responsible deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs). Yet, existing approaches often rely on heavyweight fine-tuning that is costly to update, audit, and maintain across model families. Full fine-tuning incurs substantial computational and storage overhead, while parameter-efficient methods, e.g., Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), trade efficiency for inconsistent safety gains and sensitivity to design choices. Safety intervention mechanisms reduce unsafe outputs without modifying model weights, but do not directly shape or preserve the internal representations that govern safety behavior. We present NeST, a Neuron-Selective Tuning framework for efficient post-hoc safety alignment. NeST identifies safety-relevant feed-forward neurons via activation probing on vanilla harmful and benign prompts, clusters neurons with similar activation profiles, and trains shared cluster-level updates while freezing the rest of the model. Importantly, NeST is trained only on vanilla malicious prompts, without using jailbreak-specific attack data, yet generalizes robustly to diverse jailbreaks. The learned updates are then folded into the original weights, incurring no inference-time overhead. Evaluated on 14 open-weight language and multimodal models, NeST outperforms lightweight baselines and approaches full fine-tuning robustness with significantly fewer trainable parameters. On text-only models, NeST reduces average jailbreak attack success rate from 44.5% to 1.1% while training only 0.4M parameters on average. Across multimodal settings, it reduces ASR from 55.3% to 1.1%, and for downstream fine-tuned variants, it restores safety by reducing ASR from 53.8% to 0.8%. These results show that robust, maintainable safety alignment can be achieved by concentrating adaptation on localized, functionally coherent safety structures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：NeST：用于大型语言模型安全的神经元选择性调优
安全对齐对于大型语言模型（LLMs）的负责任部署至关重要。然而，现有方法通常依赖于成本高昂的重调优，难以在模型家族中进行更新、审计和维护。完全调优会产生大量的计算和存储开销，而参数高效的方法，如低秩适应（LoRA），则在效率与安全收益不一致和对设计选择敏感之间进行权衡。安全干预机制在不修改模型权重的情况下减少不安全输出，但并未直接塑造或保留影响安全行为的内部表示。 我们提出了NeST，一种用于高效事后安全对齐的神经元选择性调优框架。NeST通过对普通有害和良性提示的激活探测，识别与安全相关的前馈神经元，聚类具有相似激活特征的神经元，并在冻结模型其余部分的同时训练共享的聚类级更新。重要的是，NeST仅在普通恶意提示上进行训练，而不使用特定于越狱的攻击数据，但能够稳健地推广到多种越狱场景。学习到的更新随后被折叠到原始权重中，不会增加推理时的开销。在14个开放权重的语言和多模态模型上进行评估，NeST的表现优于轻量级基线，并以显著更少的可训练参数接近完全调优的鲁棒性。在仅文本模型上，NeST将平均越狱攻击成功率从44.5%降低到1.1%，同时平均仅训练0.4M参数。在多模态设置中，它将ASR从55.3%降低到1.1%，对于下游微调变体，它通过将ASR从53.8%降低到0.8%来恢复安全。这些结果表明，通过集中适应于局部、功能一致的安全结构，可以实现稳健、可维护的安全对齐。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for safety alignment in the deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs), highlighting the limitations of existing methods that either require extensive fine-tuning or compromise safety effectiveness. Traditional approaches, such as full fine-tuning and Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), either incur high computational costs or yield inconsistent safety improvements. The proposed NeST (Neuron-Selective Tuning) framework offers a novel solution by focusing on safety-relevant neurons identified through activation probing, allowing for efficient post-hoc safety alignment without modifying the entire model. This method is well-motivated as it generalizes effectively to various malicious prompts while maintaining low computational overhead. The contribution of the paper lies in demonstrating that NeST can significantly reduce the average success rate of jailbreak attacks across multiple models, achieving a reduction from 44.5% to 1.1% for text-only models and from 55.3% to 1.1% for multimodal settings, while training only a small number of parameters, thus supporting the goal of robust and maintainable safety alignment.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLM）部署中安全对齐的关键需求，强调了现有方法的局限性，如全量微调资源密集，以及低秩适应（LoRA）等参数高效技术在安全一致性上的妥协。提出的NeST（神经元选择性调优）框架通过激活探测识别和调优与安全相关的神经元，提供了一种新颖的方法，实现高效的后期安全对齐，而无需修改整个模型。该方法的动机明确，旨在增强安全性，同时最小化计算成本。本文的贡献在于证明NeST能够显著降低各种模型的越狱攻击成功率，在仅训练少量参数的情况下，文本模型的成功率从44.5%降至1.1%，多模态设置下从55.3%降至1.1%，从而支持了实现稳健和可维护的安全对齐的目标。
When Behavioral Safety Evaluation Fails: A Representation-Level Perspective
Authors: Enyi Jiang, Anders Gjølbye, Yibo Jacky Zhang, Sanmi Koyejo
First: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) safety has often been evaluated at the behavior level, which provides limited evidence of internal robustness, as these evaluations target outputs rather than representation-level vulnerability under intervention. We formalize this discrepancy as the audit gap: the difference between behavioral safety and robustness under intervention. To study this gap, we construct dissociated models that preserve safe outward behavior while remaining vulnerable in the latent space. We introduce an intervention-based evaluation framework to test model robustness through soft interventions in parameter and latent spaces, including harmful fine-tuning and layer-wise latent perturbations. To formalize the evaluation, we propose the Latent Vulnerability Score (LVS) to measure how easily harmful behavior can be elicited by bounded latent perturbations. Using this evaluation framework, we show that behavioral safety metrics are insufficient measures of representation-level robustness across multiple safely and unsafely aligned state-of-the-art models. Notably, dissociated models show substantially elevated LVSs despite comparable refusal behavior under harmful intervention, with intermediate representations being the most sensitive to intervention. Our results suggest that behavioral safety evaluation alone provides an incomplete picture of model robustness, motivating representation-aware audits of latent vulnerability and observable behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：行为安全评估失败时：一种表征层面的视角
大型语言模型（LLM）的安全性通常在行为层面进行评估，这提供了有限的内部稳健性证据，因为这些评估针对的是输出，而不是在干预下的表征层面脆弱性。我们将这种差异形式化为审计差距：行为安全与干预下的稳健性之间的差异。为了研究这一差距，我们构建了保持安全外部行为的分离模型，同时在潜在空间中保持脆弱性。我们引入了一种基于干预的评估框架，通过参数和潜在空间中的软干预来测试模型的稳健性，包括有害的微调和逐层潜在扰动。为了形式化评估，我们提出了潜在脆弱性评分（LVS），以衡量有害行为在有限潜在扰动下被引发的难易程度。使用该评估框架，我们表明行为安全指标不足以衡量多种安全和不安全对齐的最先进模型的表征层面稳健性。值得注意的是，尽管在有害干预下拒绝行为相当，分离模型的LVS显著升高，中间表征对干预最为敏感。我们的结果表明，仅依靠行为安全评估无法全面反映模型的稳健性，促使对潜在脆弱性和可观察行为进行表征意识审计。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the limitations of current safety evaluations for Large Language Models (LLMs), which typically focus on behavioral outputs rather than the underlying representation-level vulnerabilities that can be exploited through interventions. Previous methods have primarily assessed safety at the behavior level, failing to capture the internal robustness of models, leading to what the authors term the audit gap. The proposed approach introduces an intervention-based evaluation framework that assesses model robustness through soft interventions in parameter and latent spaces, alongside a new metric called the Latent Vulnerability Score (LVS) to quantify susceptibility to harmful behavior. The study demonstrates that existing behavioral safety metrics do not adequately reflect representation-level robustness, revealing that dissociated models can exhibit high LVSs while maintaining similar refusal behaviors under harmful interventions. This highlights the need for representation-aware audits to provide a more comprehensive understanding of model safety and robustness.
本文探讨了当前大型语言模型（LLMs）安全评估的局限性，现有评估通常侧重于行为输出，而忽视了可通过干预利用的潜在表示级脆弱性。以往的方法主要评估行为安全，导致对模型鲁棒性的理解不完整，因为它们未考虑行为安全与表示级鲁棒性之间的审计差距。提出的方法引入了一种基于干预的评估框架，通过对参数和潜在空间的软干预来测试模型鲁棒性，并提出潜在脆弱性评分（LVS）来量化对有害行为的易感性。研究结果表明，传统的行为安全指标不足以评估表示级鲁棒性，分离模型在有害干预下表现出更高的LVS，尽管拒绝行为相似。该研究通过强调需要进行表示感知审计，以更好地评估LLMs中的潜在脆弱性和可观察行为，为该领域做出了贡献。
PreAct-Bench: Benchmarking Predictive Monitoring in LLMs
Authors: Hainiu Xu, Italo Luis da Silva, Jiangnan Ye, Yuhao Wang, Wei Liu, Linyi Yang, Jonathan Richard Schwarz, Nicola Paoletti, Yulan He, Hanqi Yan
First: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PreAct-Bench：大语言模型预测监控基准测试
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被部署为能够执行多步骤行动轨迹以实现特定目标的自主代理。虽然现有的安全研究集中在检测完整轨迹中的不道德行为，但这种范式在根本上是回顾性的：它仅在伤害发生后识别出伤害。在这项工作中，我们研究了一个关键但被忽视的安全任务，我们称之为预测监控：仅给定部分行动轨迹，模型能否推断出它是否会在显性行动执行之前以不道德的行动告终？为了支持这一任务，我们提出了PreAct-Bench，这是一个涵盖五个领域的1,000对伦理和不伦理行动轨迹的基准测试。我们使用我们的Prefix Foresight F1指标评估了一系列LLMs、安全护栏模型和潜在探测方法在不同的行动轨迹分数下的表现。结果表明，尽管人类表现出良好的性能，但即使对于强大的模型，预测监控仍然具有挑战性，突显了LLM安全中未来导向风险推理的必要性。

Previous methods have primarily concentrated on retrospective analysis of complete trajectories, which only detects harm after it has happened, thus lacking proactive measures. TamperBench: Systematically Stress-Testing LLM Safety Under Fine-Tuning and Tampering
Authors: Saad Hossain, Tom Tseng, Punya Syon Pandey, Samanvay Vajpayee, Matthew Kowal, Nayeema Nonta, Samuel Simko, Stephen Casper, Zhijing Jin, Kellin Pelrine, Sirisha Rambhatla
First: 2026-02-06T18:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T23:27:30+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 15 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As increasingly capable open-weight large language models (LLMs) are deployed, improving their tamper resistance against unsafe modifications, whether accidental or intentional, becomes critical to minimize risks. However, there is no standard approach to evaluate tamper resistance. Varied datasets, metrics, and tampering configurations make it difficult to compare safety, utility, and robustness across different models and defenses. To address this, we introduce TamperBench, the first unified framework to systematically evaluate the tamper resistance of LLMs. TamperBench (i) curates a repository of state-of-the-art weight-space fine-tuning attacks, latent-space representation attacks, and alignment-stage defenses; (ii) enables realistic adversarial evaluation through systematic hyperparameter sweeps per attack-model pair; and (iii) provides both safety and utility evaluations. We use TamperBench to evaluate 21 open-weight LLMs, including defense-augmented variants, across nine tampering threats using standardized safety and capability metrics with hyperparameter sweeps per model-attack pair. The results provide insights including effects of post-training on tamper resistance, that jailbreak-tuning is typically the most severe attack, and that current alignment-stage defenses largely fail to withstand attack sweeps. Code is available at https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench.
中文标题/摘要

随着越来越强大的开放权重大型语言模型（LLM）的部署，提高其对意外或故意不安全修改的抗篡改能力变得至关重要，以最小化风险。然而，目前没有标准的方法来评估抗篡改能力。不同的数据集、指标和篡改配置使得比较不同模型和防御的安全性、实用性和鲁棒性变得困难。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了TamperBench，这是第一个统一框架，用于系统性评估LLM的抗篡改能力。TamperBench (i) 汇集了最先进的权重空间微调攻击、潜在空间表示攻击和对齐阶段防御的库；(ii) 通过对每个攻击-模型对进行系统的超参数搜索，实现现实的对抗性评估；(iii) 提供安全性和实用性评估。我们使用TamperBench评估了21个开放权重LLM，包括增强防御的变体，针对九种篡改威胁使用标准化的安全性和能力指标，并对每个模型-攻击对进行超参数搜索。结果提供了包括后训练对抗篡改能力的影响、越狱微调通常是最严重的攻击，以及当前对齐阶段防御在抵御攻击时大多失败的见解。代码可在https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench获取。

When Autoregressive Consistency Hurts Safety Alignment
Authors: Bochen Lyu, Yiyang Jia, Xiaohao Cai, Zhanxing Zhu
First: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00
Comments: 21 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment in large language models (LLMs) is fragile in part because it is often shallow: fine-tuning mainly reshapes the model's behavior near the first few output tokens. We argue that this phenomenon can be understood through autoregressive consistency, the tendency of next-token prediction to preserve and extend the current response trajectory consistently. By analyzing the learning dynamics of safety alignment, we show that autoregressive consistency can concentrate alignment updates on early tokens, offering a mechanistic explanation for shallow safety alignment. The same mechanism also predicts a broader class of attacks on LLMs: attacks that induce harmful continuation states at arbitrary positions in the output trajectory. As a concrete example, we introduce random insertion attack, which inserts a short harmful span into an otherwise safe refusal trajectory and exploits autoregressive consistency to sustain the resulting harmful branch, thereby bypassing safety alignment. Notably, a short harmful span can redirect the generation to be harmful even after a long refusal prefix, highlighting autoregressive consistency as a potential broader failure mechanism. This suggests that safety alignment should also break harmful autoregressive consistency throughout the output trajectory. We therefore propose adversarial safety alignment, an initial framework based on worst-case harmful continuation states, and instantiate it with random worst-insertion training. Overall, our results suggest that autoregressive consistency should be treated as a central consideration in both safety alignment and attack design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归一致性如何损害安全对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐脆弱，部分原因在于其通常较浅：微调主要重塑模型在前几个输出标记附近的行为。我们认为，这一现象可以通过自回归一致性来理解，即下一个标记预测保持并延续当前响应轨迹的一致性倾向。通过分析安全对齐的学习动态，我们表明自回归一致性可以将对齐更新集中在早期标记上，为浅层安全对齐提供了机制性解释。同样的机制也预测了一类更广泛的对LLMs的攻击：在输出轨迹的任意位置诱导有害延续状态的攻击。作为具体例子，我们引入随机插入攻击，该攻击将一个短的有害片段插入到原本安全的拒绝轨迹中，并利用自回归一致性来维持由此产生的有害分支，从而绕过安全对齐。值得注意的是，一个短的有害片段可以在长拒绝前缀后重新引导生成变得有害，突显自回归一致性作为潜在的更广泛失败机制。这表明安全对齐也应打破输出轨迹中有害的自回归一致性。因此，我们提出了对抗性安全对齐，这是一个基于最坏情况有害延续状态的初步框架，并通过随机最坏插入训练进行实例化。总体而言，我们的结果表明，自回归一致性应被视为安全对齐和攻击设计中的核心考虑。

Black-box, Adaptive, Efficient, Transferable, Harmful, Applicable... Attacks Are All You Need to Break LLMs
Authors: Vincent Limbach, Jonas Dornbusch, David Lüdke, Stephan Günnemann, Leo Schwinn
First: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurately evaluating adversarial robustness is a longstanding challenge. A flawed attack design can inflate robustness estimates, making deployment risk assessment and defense comparison unreliable. Historically, standardized attacks such as AutoAttack have largely resolved this for image classifiers, providing a reliable evaluation baseline for systematic comparison across defenses. However, no equivalent exists for LLM jailbreak evaluation yet, where designing such an attack is considerably more difficult. A reliable attack must, among other things, be black-box compatible, applicable to arbitrary defense pipelines, and efficient, which no existing method jointly satisfies. We introduce Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), a masked diffusion language model attacker trained via iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, requiring only black-box access to the target. The same method can be used without modification as a strong adaptive attack on individual behaviors, or as an efficient amortized policy that transfers to held-out behaviors and unseen target models without fine-tuning. Even against layered defenses, such as a Circuit Breaker-trained model combined with an auxiliary detector, IHO improves attack success considerably over state-of-the-art approaches, without any defense-specific adaptation. Our results position IHO as a practical step toward the kind of standardized jailbreak evaluation that has improved reliability in the past. Code and models are available on GitHub and Hugging Face.
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑箱、自适应、高效、可转移、有害、适用……攻击是破解LLM所需的一切
准确评估对抗鲁棒性一直是一个长期挑战。设计不当的攻击可能会夸大鲁棒性估计，使得部署风险评估和防御比较不可靠。历史上，标准化攻击如AutoAttack在图像分类器中基本解决了这一问题，为系统比较提供了可靠的评估基准。然而，目前尚无等效的LLM越狱评估标准，设计这样的攻击要困难得多。一个可靠的攻击必须在许多方面兼容黑箱，适用于任意防御管道，并且高效，而现有方法没有一个能够共同满足这些要求。我们引入了间接有害优化（IHO），这是一种通过迭代偏好优化训练的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者，仅需对目标进行黑箱访问。相同的方法可以在不修改的情况下作为对个体行为的强自适应攻击，或作为一种高效的摊销策略，能够转移到保留行为和未见目标模型上，而无需微调。即使面对分层防御，如与辅助检测器结合的电路断路器训练模型，IHO在攻击成功率上显著超越了最先进的方法，而无需任何特定于防御的适应。我们的结果将IHO定位为朝着标准化越狱评估的实用步骤，这在过去提高了可靠性。代码和模型可在GitHub和Hugging Face上获取。

D-Judge: Disrupting Multi-Turn Jailbreaks using Semantics-Preserving Output Rewriting
Authors: Huanli Gong, Zhipeng Wei, Yu Fu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Ananya Gupta, Yue Dong, N. Benjamin Erichson
First: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 43rd International Conference on Machine Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks pose a growing threat to large language model (LLM) safety because they exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to iteratively refine prompts toward harmful goals. Existing defenses largely detect or block unsafe content at individual turns or at the final response, leaving the judge-driven refinement loop intact and allowing attackers to extract informative feedback from intermediate interactions. We introduce D-Judge, a semantics-preserving output rewriting defense that intervenes directly in this loop by rewriting the victim LLM's responses before they are evaluated by the attacker's judge. By misaligning the judge's feedback signal without changing the meaning of the original response, D-Judge derails the attacker's prompt-refinement process, causing subsequent queries to be optimized against a distorted signal of attack progress. To improve D-Judge's ability to produce such rewrites, we construct a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs that induce different judge-assigned harmfulness scores, and use it for supervised fine-tuning followed by direct preference optimization. Experiments on HarmBench show that D-Judge reduces the success rate of state-of-the-art multi-turn jailbreaks while preserving performance on benign benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：D-Judge：通过语义保持输出重写来破坏多轮越狱攻击
多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）的安全构成日益严重的威胁，因为它们利用辅助评判模型的反馈，迭代地优化提示以达到有害目标。现有防御主要在单个回合或最终响应中检测或阻止不安全内容，保持评判驱动的优化循环不变，使攻击者能够从中间交互中提取有用反馈。我们提出了D-Judge，这是一种语义保持输出重写防御，直接干预这一循环，通过在攻击者的评判之前重写受害者LLM的响应。通过在不改变原始响应含义的情况下使评判的反馈信号失真，D-Judge使攻击者的提示优化过程偏离轨道，导致后续查询针对扭曲的攻击进展信号进行优化。为了提高D-Judge生成此类重写的能力，我们构建了一个语义等价响应对的数据集，该数据集引发不同的评判分配有害性评分，并用于监督微调，随后进行直接偏好优化。在HarmBench上的实验表明，D-Judge在保持良性基准性能的同时，降低了最先进的多轮越狱攻击的成功率。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing threat of multi-turn jailbreak attacks on large language models (LLMs), which exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to refine harmful prompts. Previous methods primarily focused on detecting or blocking unsafe content at individual turns or final responses, failing to disrupt the iterative feedback loop that attackers exploit. The proposed D-Judge approach differs by intervening directly in this loop, rewriting the LLM's responses to misalign the judge's feedback without altering the original meaning, thereby disrupting the attacker's prompt-refinement process. This method is well-motivated as it targets the core mechanism of the attack. The paper contributes a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs for supervised fine-tuning and demonstrates through experiments on HarmBench that D-Judge significantly reduces the success rate of advanced multi-turn jailbreaks while maintaining performance on benign tasks.
